[ bhāṣyam‌ ] 
na॒viparya̭yopādī ca | vastuśunyakhe'pi śabdajñānamāhāsyani- 
bandhano bhyavah‌ro dṛśyate | tyathā--““ cetanyaṃ puruṣya svahūpam‌" iti |

vṛttiḥ, ya॒thā --“ vacetrasya gauḥ” iti |

virodhādvāṣyate, tathā vikalpaḥ | pramāṇapryayaguṇamāvadeva || 


tasmādrastuśūnyalagrahaṇina rabdajñānānupātilamrahaṇena ca parasparasaṃbandhena

sṛte: kevalānubhūtāspadalavāt‌ ||

tirekopanibandhane vyapadeśo na syāt‌--papuraprasya caitanyama! iti | tathā cemame- 
vādhapupāścilaya śabdavidā vārtikakareṇoktam‌-- “siddhaṃ tu bhyapadeśivadvāvāt‌)'

iti bhyapadera vṛttiḥ ||
